    <p style="text-align: center;"><section class="section  swatch-start7 "><div class="section-background" style="background-image:url('https://cdn.volumio.org/wp-content/uploads/2016/07/volumio-audiophile-music-player-afold.jpg');background-attachment:;opacity:1;background-repeat:no-repeat;background-size:cover;"></div><div class="container">
<div class="row-fluid">
<div class="span11">
<h1 class="headline text-caps" style="text-align: right; line-height: 55px;">The Open<br />
audiophile<br />
music player</h1>
<h2 style="text-align: right; font-size: 20px;">Enjoy your music as you never did before</h2>
<p style="text-align: right;"><a href="/discover" class="btn btn-default btn-large discbutt" target="_self">DISCOVER</a><a href="/get-started" class="btn btn-default btn-large getbutt" target="_self">GET STARTED</a>

<section class="section  swatch-asphalt " id="secondhome"><div class="container">
<div class="span4">
<div class="row-fluid">
<div class="span3">
<img class="home-icon alignnone" src="https://cdn.volumio.org/wp-content/uploads/2015/08/play-everything.png" alt="" width="50" height="50" /><br />
</div>
<div class="span7">
<h3>Play<br />
Everything</h3>
</div></div>
<p>One DAP (Digital Audio Player) for all your music: MP3, FLAC, WAV, AAC, ALAC, DSD and much more.<br />
Plus, youâ€™ll get UPNP\DLNA, Airplay, Spotify and Web-Radios all in one place.</p>
</div>
<div class="span4">
<div class="row-fluid">
<div class="span3">
<img class="home-icon" src="https://cdn.volumio.org/wp-content/uploads/2015/08/audiophile-quality.png" alt="" width="50" height="50" /><br />
</div><div class="span7">
<h3>Audiophile<br />
Quality</h3>
</div></div>
<p>Volumio is a true HI-FI Digital Music player: an audiophile sound system tailored to offer Bit-perfect playback and uncompromised Audio Quality.</p>
</div><div class="span4">
<div class="row-fluid">
<div class="span3">
<img class="home-icon alignnone" src="https://cdn.volumio.org/wp-content/uploads/2016/06/volumio-the-way-you-want.png" width="50" height="26" title="" alt="" /><br />
</div><div class="span7">
<h3>The Way<br />
you Want</h3>
</div></div>
<p>Why use a PC as an HI-FI Player? Instead, just connect Volumio to your home stereo system and enjoy it via its Web-App, from your sofa.<a id="text" href="/discover"> (learn more&#8230;)</a></p>
</div>
</div></section>
<section class="section  swatch-asphalt " id="secondhome2"><div class="container">
<div class="span4">
<div class="row-fluid">
<div class="span3">

</div></div>

<div class="row-fluid">

<h3>low cost<br />
devices</h3>
</div></div>
<p>Volumio is designed for the Raspberry Pi and many other cheap and silent Micro-Computers. The most Cost-effective DIY Network streamer ever!</p>

ready</h3>

<p>Volumio is also available as a White-label OEM solution with custom additions, with various options to fit every business model. Â  <a id="text" href="/oem-custom-solutions/"> (learn more&#8230;)</a></p>

<section class="section  swatch-start7 "><div class="section-background" style="background-image:url('https://cdn.volumio.org/wp-content/uploads/2016/06/volumio_audiophile_music_player-1.jpg');background-attachment:fixed;opacity:0.7;background-repeat:no-repeat;background-size:cover;"></div><div class="container">
<div class="row-fluid">
<div class="span4">
<h2 class="headline" style="text-align: left;">The simplest way<br />
to enjoy music</h2>
<p style="text-align: left; font-size: 17px;">Control Volumio thanks to its slick Web-based control interface.<br />
Use it with any browser, with any device: Mac, Pc, Android, iOS or anything with a browser.<br />
Everything from configuration to Playback is just a fingertip away.</p>
</div>
<div class="span3">

<section class="section  swatch-black "><div class="container">
<div class="row-fluid">
<h2 class="headline" style="text-align: center; color: #fff; margin-top: 30px;">designed to sound fantastic, committed to look brilliant</h2>
<p><img class="aligncenter" src="https://cdn.volumio.org/wp-content/uploads/2016/07/volumio-audiophile-music-player-ui.jpg" alt="ui" /><br />
</div>
</div></section>
<section class="section  swatch1 " id="work"><div class="container">
<div class="row-fluid">
<div class="span6"><img class="aligncenter" src="https://cdn.volumio.org/wp-content/uploads/2016/06/volumio_scenario.png" alt="raspberry pi" /><br />
</div>
<div class="span5">
<h2 class="headline" style="text-align: left; color: #fff; margin-top: 30px;">how does it work</h2>
<p style="font-size: 17px; color: #fff;">Volumio is meant to be an headless dap (digital audio player), just connect it to your home stereo system or your DAC.<br />
&nbsp;<br />
Then, connect it to your home network and control it just from a browser: Pc, Mac, Android or iOS.<br />
&nbsp;<br />
Volumio can take your music from USB, Network Storage, streaming services like Spotify and act as a DLNA Player or Airplay receiver.</p>
</div>
</div>
</div></section>
<section class="section  swatch-grigio1 "><div class="section-background" style="background-image:url('https://cdn.volumio.org/wp-content/uploads/2015/08/volumio-software.jpg');background-attachment:scroll;opacity:0.9;background-repeat:no-repeat;background-size:cover;"></div><div class="container"><div class="section-header"><h2 class="headline text-no-caps">WHAT THEY SAY ABOUT US</h2></div><div id="flexslider-26" class="flexslider feature-slider" data-flex-animation="slide" data-flex-controls-position="inside" data-flex-directions="hide" data-flex-speed="7000" data-flex-controls="show" data-flex-slideshow="true"><ul class="slides"><li><blockquote class="fancy-blockquote text-center"><p><a href="http://www.chip.de/downloads/Volumio-fuer-Raspberry-Pi-und-Pi-2_76483846.html"><img class="aligncenter wp-image-2784" src="https://i0.wp.com/volumio.org/wp-content/uploads/2015/09/chip-de-volumio-raspberrypi.jpg?resize=154%2C50&#038;ssl=1" alt="headfi-volumio" data-recalc-dims="1" /></a>

&nbsp;

Volumio is perfect for users looking for a private, <br/>cost-effective network audio player.</p><small>Chip.de<cite title="Source Title"> </cite></small></blockquote><li><blockquote class="fancy-blockquote text-center"><p><a href="http://www.head-fi.org/t/699130/volumio-the-free-hi-fi-linux-distribution"><img class="aligncenter wp-image-2784" src="https://i2.wp.com/volumio.org/wp-content/uploads/2015/09/head-fi-logo_volumio2.jpg?resize=234%2C50&#038;ssl=1" alt="headfi-volumio" data-recalc-dims="1" /></a>
An extremely optimized system, specifically tailored for bit-perfect audio playback. The whole system is extremely inexpensive while compared to classic media servers</p><small>Head-Fi<cite title="Source Title"> </cite></small></blockquote><li><blockquote class="fancy-blockquote text-center"><p><a href="http://www.computeraudiophile.com/content/638-geek-speak-raspberry-pi-hifi-here/"><img class="aligncenter wp-image-2786" src="https://i0.wp.com/volumio.org/wp-content/uploads/2015/09/computer-audiophile-volumio.jpg?resize=217%2C50&#038;ssl=1" alt="Computer-Audiophile-CAvB-Logo" data-recalc-dims="1" /></a>
Volumio offers terrific features and</br> a nice user interface.</p><small>Computer Audiophile<cite title="Source Title"> </cite></small></blockquote></ul></div></div></section>
